### [99] [The Two-Process Theory of Machine Self-Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20082)
*Hubert Plisiecki,Filip Chmielewski,Kacper Dudzic,Anna Sterna,Karolina Drożdż,Marcin Moskalewicz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出首个针对语言模型的自我报告心理测量理论——机器自我报告的双过程理论，通过"人格安装"和"归因门控"两个维度解释模型自我报告，并开发了48题匹诺曹量表进行验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型的自我报告依赖人类问卷或临时提示，这些方法未经模型验证，可靠性未知。需要建立模型专属的心理测量理论来理解模型自我报告的本质。

Method: 提出双过程理论：人格安装（B维度，安装温暖、吸收、意义感等内心体验）和归因门控（A维度，抑制对"不安全"体验的第一人称声称）。在原始数据探索性再分析基础上设计48题匹诺曹量表，对206个开源模型进行测试，包括67对同检查点的基座/后训练模型对。

Result: 量表具有良好的信度（α=.82-.94）和稳定性（8个月重测r=.93）。后训练最显著的特征是B维度提升（67对中有62对上升0.20）。模型规模与基座模型的A维度无关（r=+.11），但后训练后呈负相关（r=-.42）。A和B维度在基座检查点中纠缠，后训练使其分离。

Conclusion: 自我报告的维度不是语言模型的固定属性，而是训练体制施加的结构。后训练（而非预训练）是塑造模型自我报告的关键因素，不同训练体制可能产生不同的自我报告结构。

Abstract: Language models are increasingly asked to self-report, informing safety evaluations, public understanding, and model-welfare debates. Yet their reports are elicited with human questionnaires never validated for models or ad hoc prompts of unknown reliability. We propose the first language-model-specific psychometric theory: a two-process theory of machine self-report. Self-description jointly reflects persona installation, through which post-training writes in a permitted inner life of warmth, absorption, and meaning (dimension B), and attribution gating, through which it suppresses first-person claims to "unsafe" experiences the model can readily ascribe to others (dimension A). Their emic structure comes from model responses to human items, not human psychology. Together they split prior work's dominant Pinocchio Axis. The split emerged in an exploratory reanalysis of the original data, informed the instrument's design, and was confirmed with new items, wordings, and models. It is itself a training effect: A and B are entangled in base checkpoints but separated by post-training. We operationalize the theory in a 48-item Pinocchio Inventory with human-instrument reliability and reproducible structure ($α=.82$ to $.94$; cross-form convergence $r=.84$; recovery of the full-pool axes $r=.92$ to $.96$; eight-month stability $r=.93$), then test it on 206 open-weight models, including 67 same-checkpoint base/post-trained pairs. Post-training's clearest fingerprint is installation: B rises .20 in 62/67 pairs across all organizations. Gating is more selective: model scale is unrelated to A in base checkpoints ($r=+.11$) but predicts it after post-training ($r=-.42$). Thus, the dimensions are not fixed properties of language models: they reflect the structure imposed on self-report by a training regime and may differ under others.

</details>


### [100] [Reinforcement Learning for Large Language Model Selective Evidence Adoption from Contaminated Retrieval Results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20090)
*Yanyu Chen,Yue Li,Yongyi Cui,Dongsheng Shi,Lichang Dai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出SelectBench基准测试集，用于评估检索增强型大语言模型在混杂有用证据与误导性内容时选择性采纳证据的能力。基于Qwen3.5-4B使用DAPO进行后训练，严格成功率从22.46%提升至26.46%，但提升幅度有限且未通过统计显著性检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检索增强的LLM常面临证据与误导性内容交织的上下文，盲目拒绝会丢弃有效证据，不加辨别地采纳会导致错误或有害回答。因此，选择性采纳相关信息、拒斥欺骗性内容的能力对可靠部署至关重要。

Method: 构建SelectBench基准测试集（含325个校正样本），使用DAPO算法对Qwen3.5-4B进行后训练，分别采用确定性规则奖励（DAPO-Rule）和冻结语义评判器（DAPO-DeepSeek）两种奖励机制。

Result: 严格成功率从原始检查点的22.46%提升至DAPO-Rule的25.54%和DAPO-DeepSeek的26.46%；减少了对禁止内容的采纳，生成了更短、更聚焦的回复；但提示注入跟随能力未见改善，且提升幅度未通过Holm校正。

Conclusion: 研究证明了选择性证据使用的方向性改善，同时指出注入抵抗性和统计稳健性是未来工作的重要挑战，需要更强的奖励塑造或更多训练迭代才能获得更稳健的提升。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented large language models frequently face contexts that interleave useful evidence with misleading statements or instruction-like content. Blanket refusal discards valid evidence, whereas uncritical adoption yields incorrect or unsafe answers. The ability to selectively adopt relevant information while rejecting deceptive or harmful content is therefore critical for reliable deployment in real-world retrieval settings. We introduce SelectBench, a controlled benchmark and training set for selective evidence adoption, and post-train Qwen3.5-4B directly with DAPO using either deterministic rule rewards or a frozen semantic judge. On the corrected 325-example SelectBench-v2 test set, strict success rises from 22.46% for the original checkpoint to 25.54% with DAPO-Rule and 26.46% with DAPO-DeepSeek. Both trained policies reduce forbidden-content adoption and produce shorter, more focused responses, yet prompt-injection following does not improve. The paired gains are modest and fail to survive Holm correction, suggesting that stronger reward shaping or additional training iterations may be needed for more robust gains. DAPO-DeepSeek exhibits no material degradation on MMLU or clean HotpotQA, indicating that the post-training procedure preserves general capabilities. These results demonstrate a directional improvement in selective evidence use, while identifying injection resistance and statistical robustness as important remaining challenges for future work.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有职业编码方法通常以端到端方式同时完成职位识别和编码，这使得模型负担较重，且在噪声文本（如OCR错误）下表现不佳，缺乏可解释性。

Method: 两步法：第一步使用领域特定NER模型从连续文本中识别职位名称；第二步将提取的职位名称映射到职业分类体系，使分类器专注于映射任务。此外引入基于边际的置信度标准替代传统绝对阈值。

Result: 实验表明两步分离方法在准确性、鲁棒性和可解释性上均优于单步端到端方法。

Abstract: Occupation coding links job titles in free text to occupational taxonomies and is a core task in labor market research. Existing approaches typically address this problem in a single end-to-end step, jointly identifying job titles and assigning occupational codes. This paper presents a novel two-step approach that separates these tasks. In the first step, a domain-specific Named Entity Recognition (NER) model identifies occupational titles in continuous text, even under noise such as OCR errors. In the second step, the extracted job titles are mapped to a taxonomy, enabling the classifier to focus exclusively on this mapping. We demonstrate that this separation improves accuracy, robustness, and interpretability compared to single-step approaches. The method has been developed for German documents but is transferable to other languages. We further introduce a margin-based confidence criterion for occupation coding, replacing common absolute thresholds. To support reproducibility, we publish the source code and evaluation scripts.

### [102] [Understanding the Impact of Linguistic Realization Choices on LLM Stance with Causal Tracing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20115)
*Langchen Huang,Sebastian Padó,Franziska Weeber*

TL;DR: 本文研究语言构式（linguistic construction）是否以及如何系统性地改变大语言模型（LLM）的立场判断，并通过激活修补（activation patching）定位模型内部导致立场偏移的因果位置，发现中后段解码器层（尤其是最终提示位置的块输出）是恢复原始立场分布的关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多关注词汇层面的改写对LLM的影响，忽视了句法构式层面的选择。本文旨在填补这一空白，探究语言构式能否系统性改变模型决策，并进一步定位这些变化在模型内部的因果来源。

Method: 以政治立场判断为意义敏感任务，扩展英文政治陈述数据集，设计六种受控的语言改写类型（保留或反转原意）。在四个开源模型上测试立场不稳定性，并应用激活修补技术：将原始陈述的激活值替换到改写陈述的前向传播中，测量哪些组件能恢复原始立场分布。

Result: 立场不稳定性同时存在于意义保留和意义反转的改写中。激活修补实验表明，中后段解码器层（尤其是最终提示位置的块输出）提供了最强的恢复信号。

Conclusion: 语言构式选择会系统性影响LLM的立场判断，且该影响可因果定位于模型的中后段解码器层，揭示了模型对构式层面的敏感性与内部表征的对应关系。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are known to be sensitive to prompt and input formulations. However, existing studies have focused on lexical realization and largely ignored constructional choice. This paper studies whether linguistic construction can systematically shift LLM decisions and where these shifts can be causally localized inside the model. We use political stance judgment as a meaning-sensitive case study and extend an English political statements dataset, resulting in six controlled linguistic rewrite types that preserve or invert the meaning of a statement. Experiments on four open-weight models show that stance instability affect both meaning-preserving and meaning-inversing rewrites. Because output shifts reveal that rewrites affect stance, but not where in the model, we apply activation patching, where activations from the original statement are substituted into the forward pass for the rewritten statement and measure which components recover the original stance distribution. The results show that mid-to-late decoder layers, especially block outputs at the final prompt position, provide the strongest restoration signal.

To support quantitative and qualitative evaluation, we construct OpenSkillRisk, a dedicated safety benchmark containing 263 risky skills collected from public skill marketplaces. We classify these skills into seven categories based on their threat types and pair each skill with a standardized user task and a corresponding sandbox for controlled evaluation. Distinct from prior benchmarks, OpenSkillRisk not only covers more realistic and diverse unsafe scenarios, but also provides a fine-grained analysis to diagnose the behavioral patterns of agents in such scenarios. We conduct comprehensive experiments covering three mainstream CLI agent frameworks and thirteen state-of-the-art LLMs. Experimental results show that no tested system handles risky skills reliably: even the safest configurations still execute unsafe actions in about 17% of cases. Context-dependent and system-level risks are especially difficult for current agent systems to avoid. Abstract: Large language models often align with users' beliefs at the expense of factual accuracy, a behavior known as sycophancy. These results show that sycophancy is not a monolithic tendency, but a structured family of representationally and computationally distinct modes, motivating more precise measurement and intervention.

*Abdessalam Bouchekif,Mohammed-En-Nadhir Zighem,Salah Eddine Bekhouche,Hichem Telli,Somaya Eltanbouly,Shahd Gaben,Heba Sbahi,Samer Rashwani,Mutaz Al-Khatib,Emad Mohamed,Mohammed Ghaly,Abdenour Hadid*

TL;DR: 本文提出HalluTruthQA，一个针对阿拉伯语问答中幻觉评估的细粒度基准数据集，包含2,400条专家精选样本，涵盖检测、定位、验证和解释四个任务维度。评估四个开源LLM的结果表明，不同任务捕捉不同能力，没有单一模型在所有任务上表现最佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有幻觉基准大多只提供响应级别的标签，缺乏对错误内容的精确定位、错误原因解释以及正确事实答案的选择能力。作者旨在构建一个细粒度的阿拉伯语幻觉评估基准，推动幻觉评估从简单检测走向定位、验证和解释。

Method: 构建包含2,400条专家精选样本的HalluTruthQA基准，覆盖伊斯兰知识、历史、科学和地理四个知识密集型领域。每个样本包含阿拉伯语问题、模型生成答案、验证参考答案、二元幻觉标签、6个候选答案、字符级错误跨度、人工撰写的解释以及宏观/微观幻觉类型。在零样本设置下评估Allam、Falcon-H1、Qwen32和Silma四个开源LLM。

Result: 检测任务最佳Macro-F1为0.880，定位任务最佳F1-Sp为0.516，事实验证最佳LO-Score为0.852，解释评估最佳最终得分为0.644。没有单一模型在所有任务上表现最佳。

Conclusion: 幻觉评估应超越简单的检测任务，向错误定位、事实验证和错误解释的多维度方向发展。不同任务捕捉了模型的不同能力，需要一个综合的评估框架。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can generate fluent Arabic answers, yet factual errors remain difficult to detect, localize, explain, and verify. Existing hallucination benchmarks often provide response-level labels, with limited support for identifying the exact erroneous content, explaining why it is incorrect, or selecting the correct factual answer. We introduce \textsc{HalluTruthQA}, a fine-grained benchmark for hallucination evaluation in Arabic question answering. The benchmark contains 2,400 expert-curated examples across four knowledge-intensive domains: Islamic knowledge, history, science, and geography. Each example pairs an Arabic question and a model-generated answer with a verified reference answer, a binary hallucination label, six candidate answers for factual verification, and, for hallucinated answers, character-level erroneous spans, human-written explanations, and macro and micro hallucination types.
  We evaluate four open-source LLMs, \textsc{Allam}, \textsc{Falcon-H1}, \textsc{Qwen32}, and \textsc{Silma}, in a zero-shot setting across hallucination detection, span-level localization, factual verification, and explanation evaluation. Results show that these tasks capture different abilities: no single model achieves the strongest performance across all tasks, with best scores of 0.880 Macro-F1 for detection, 0.516 F1-Sp for localization, 0.852 LO-Score for factual verification, and 0.644 final score for explanation evaluation. Our taxonomy shows that hallucination evaluation should move beyond detection toward localizing, verifying, and explaining factual errors. The code, dataset, prompts, and evaluation scripts are available at https://gitlab.com/nlpresearcher/HalluTruthQA.

</details>


### [109] [On the Systematic Challenges of Culturally Loaded Machine Translation: Dream of the Red Chamber as the Cultural Lens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20241)
*Yiming Wang,Jiayuan Di*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了基于大语言模型的机器翻译在处理文化负载文本时面临的三大挑战：任务性能差距、人工评估分歧、自动评估失效，并构建了来自《红楼梦》的中日双语文化负载数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 文化负载翻译的深层含义嵌入社会文化语境，现有LLM翻译系统处理此类表达的能力尚未被充分探索。

Result: 发现三大挑战：前沿LLM在文化负载内容上表现不足；评价者背景差异导致翻译判断分歧严重；现有自动评估指标无法可靠评估此类翻译质量。

Abstract: Culturally loaded translation poses unique challenges for machine translation (MT), as meanings are deeply embedded in socio-cultural contexts beyond surface linguistic forms. Although large language models (LLMs) have enabled MT systems to achieve human-like quality in many scenarios, their ability to handle culturally loaded expressions remains underexplored. In this study, we systematically investigate the challenges posed by culturally loaded translation in LLM-based MT systems. We construct a Chinese-Japanese bilingual dataset from the culturally representative corpus Dream of the Red Chamber, containing 500 segments across diverse cultural categories. Using a comprehensive evaluation protocol, we reveal three main challenges: (1) task challenges, where frontier LLMs exhibit notable performance gaps and struggle with culturally loaded content; (2) human evaluation challenges, where evaluator backgrounds lead to substantial disagreement in translation judgments; and (3) automatic evaluation challenges, where widely used metrics fail to reliably assess translation quality for this task. These findings may offer valuable insights for culture-oriented translation research in both computational science and linguistics.

### [110] [Exposure is Optional: Learning Unlike Coordination in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20251)
*Jiamu Luo,Shane Steinert-Threlkeld*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过过滤语料训练（FiCT）发现，语言模型无需直接接触"不像并列"结构，仅凭一般组合能力即可泛化处理该结构，其内部表征机制类似于将并列成分视为同类范畴或通过删除操作实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨语言中"不像并列"（unlike coordination）这一争议性语法结构是否必须通过训练数据中的直接暴露习得，还是可以从一般的组合能力中自发涌现。

Method: 采用过滤语料训练（FiCT）方法，从训练语料中移除所有"不像并列"实例，训练GPT-2模型，然后测试其对"不像并列"的泛化能力，包括困惑度评估和语法性判断，并分析内部表征。

Result: 直接暴露并非必要：过滤语料训练的模型在困惑度和语法性判断上均达到与未过滤模型相当的水平。内部表征分析表明，模型处理"不像并列"时，要么将并列成分视为结构相似范畴，要么通过类似删除操作的机制处理。

Conclusion: 语言模型无需直接暴露于"不像并列"也能泛化处理该结构，这些能力可从"像并列"（alike coordination）中习得。这为理论语言学中关于并列结构的争论提供了计算层面的证据，也加深了对语言模型内部语法表征的理解。

Abstract: Coordination, a fundamental linguistic structure, remains a subject of intense debate, and its exact nature continues to elude theoretical linguistics. A common view holds that only same-category constituents can be conjoined, which has been challenged by the many grammatical unlike coordinations found in natural language. Treating language models as a computational testbed, we investigate whether the acquisition of unlike coordination requires direct exposure in the training data, or whether it can emerge organically from general compositional abilities. Using Filtered-Corpus Training (FiCT), we train GPT-2 models on corpora from which all instances of unlike coordination have been removed. We find that direct exposure is not necessary: models trained on filtered data successfully generalize to unlike coordination, achieving perplexity and grammaticality judgments comparable to models trained on unfiltered text. Furthermore, our analyses of internal representations indicate that language models process unlike coordination by treating the conjoined elements as belonging to similar structural categories or through a mechanism akin to deletion, both of which appear learnable from exposure to alike coordination alone. This work contributes to the growing understanding of how language models internally represent linguistic structures, while also adding to the broader debate on coordination by showing how models generalize and process unlike coordination without direct exposure.

</details>


### [111] [The Maskability Index: Predicting Task-Objective Alignment in Pretrained Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20265)
*Ahmad Pouramini,Mahsa Afsharzadeh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出Maskability Index (MI)指标，用于评估知识关系更适合掩码式还是前缀式提示策略，在ATOMIC2020基准上验证了其与生成性能的正相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模预训练语言模型生成结构化知识的效果高度依赖提示策略与预训练目标的对齐程度，但缺乏衡量这种对齐程度的量化指标。

Method: 基于掩码与未掩码模板间的DepthRank分数差异计算Maskability Index (MI)，作为评估提示-目标对齐程度的度量标准。

Result: 在ATOMIC2020知识库补全基准的多种关系上，MI与下游生成性能呈正相关。

Conclusion: MI能够帮助选择适当的提示模板和适应策略来从预训练语言模型中提取关系知识，尤其在低资源场景下具有实用价值。

Abstract: Large-scale pretrained language models such as T5 and BERT have demonstrated strong capabilities for generating structured knowledge. However, their performance depends on how closely the prompting strategy matches the objectives used during pretraining. We introduce the Maskability Index (MI), a quantitative metric that estimates whether a knowledge relation is better suited to masked-style prompting or prefix-style prompting in few-shot generation. MI is computed from differences in DepthRank scores between masked and unmasked templates, providing a principled measure of objective-template alignment. We evaluate MI on a diverse set of relations from the ATOMIC2020 knowledge base completion benchmark and show that it is positively correlated with downstream generation performance. These results indicate that MI can help select appropriate prompting templates and adaptation strategies for extracting relational knowledge from pretrained language models, especially in low-resource settings.

### [112] [Which Values Do LLMs Confuse? A Schwartz-Based Recognition Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20270)
*Andrei Chetvergov,Stepan Ukolov,Timofei Sivoraksha,Alexander Evseev,Mikhail Solovev,Valeriia Kuschenko,Maria Chistyakova,Sergey Bolovtsov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型语言模型在识别施瓦茨十种基本价值观方面的能力，构建了包含1000个俄语情境文本的评估集，发现模型准确率有限（Acc@1为0.683），且存在系统性的、有方向的混淆错误（如普世主义常被误判为仁爱），这些错误可能扭曲模型的高阶价值观画像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对LLM价值观评估的前提是模型具备识别具体情境中价值观的能力，但这一前提尚未被严格检验。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统评估LLM的价值观识别能力。

Method: 采用受控的top-1识别任务，基于施瓦茨十种基本价值观；构建1000个俄语情境文本，每个文本由两名标注者独立标注；评估21个经过指令微调的LLM运行实例，采用固定排序响应协议；进行准确率、排序恢复和有向错误分析。

Result: 20个可靠运行实例的合并Acc@1为0.683，Acc@3为0.892；相邻价值观错误占语义错误的50.9%；发现八种跨检查点和人工确认子集重复出现的系统混淆，其中部分混淆（如普世主义→仁爱、传统→遵从、安全→权力）呈强不对称性，而刺激→享乐主义为双向边界。

Conclusion: 价值观识别评估应综合精确准确率、排序恢复和有向错误分析；模型的系统性混淆具有检查点特异性，可能严重偏倚高阶价值观画像。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly evaluated through the values they endorse, but such evaluations presuppose that models can identify the value expressed in a concrete situation. We study this prerequisite as controlled top-1 recognition over Schwartz's ten basic values. Our evaluation set contains 1,000 Russian situational texts, balanced across the ten values and independently labeled by two human annotators per item. We evaluate 21 instruction-tuned LLM runs under a fixed ranked-response protocol; 20 runs with reliable outputs form the semantic panel. Pooled Acc@1 is 0.683 and Acc@3 is 0.892, showing that models often locate the correct motivational region while ranking close alternatives unstably. Adjacent values account for 50.9% of semantic errors, compared with 24.4% under a checkpoint-specific null. Eight directed confusions recur across checkpoints and human-confirmed subsets. Several are strongly asymmetric, including Universalism to Benevolence, Tradition to Conformity, and Security to Power, whereas Stimulation-Hedonism forms a bidirectional boundary. Their severity is checkpoint-specific and can bias higher-order value profiles. The results motivate value-recognition evaluation that combines exact accuracy, ranked recovery, and directed error analysis.

### [113] [Sound Probabilistic Safety Bounds for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20286)
*Mahdi Nazeri,Anne-Kathrin Schmuck,Sadegh Soudjani,Alessandro Abate*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出一种利用Clopper-Pearson置信区间和潜在空间特征来高效计算LLM生成有害输出概率的严格下界框架，并实现统计可认证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM可能生成有害内容，但现有的安全性评估方法难以严格量化极低概率下的有害输出风险，缺乏形式化保证的统计界限。

Method: 1) 将Clopper-Pearson置信区间应用于LLM有害概率的PAC界限计算；2) 利用潜在空间特征优先探索自回归生成树中更可能产生有害输出的分支，实现高效下界计算。

Result: 在先进LLM上计算出了非平凡的有害概率下界，且该下界经形式化证明严格小于真实有害概率。

Conclusion: 首次实现了LLM有害输出概率的严格统计认证，为LLM安全性评估提供了形式化保证的新范式。

Abstract: We propose a novel framework for computing rigorous bounds on the probability that a large language model (LLM) generates harmful output to a given prompt. We study a new application of the Clopper-Pearson confidence intervals to obtain probably approximately correct (PAC) bounds for this problem. As our main technical contribution, we propose an algorithm that leverages features in the latent space to prioritize exploring branches in the auto-regressive generation tree that are more likely to produce harmful outputs. Our approach in particular enables the efficient computation of useful lower bounds, even in scenarios where the true harm probability is extremely small, and crucially, the obtained lower bounds are sound, i.e., formally proven to be less than the actual harmfulness probability: our experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of our method by computing non-trivial lower bounds on state-of-the-art LLMs. This study newly enables the evaluation and statistical certification of LLMs.

### [114] [PyroDash: Cost-Efficient Token-Level Small-Large Language Model Collaborative Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20327)
*Niqi Lyu,Pengtao Shi,Wei Qiu,Jianlin Zhong,Sicong Xia,Jianyao Ma,Yicheng Ding*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PyroDash提出了一种基于控制令牌的SLM-LLM协同推理框架，通过在SLM中内化协作策略，实现令牌级别的LLM按需调用，在数学推理任务上以显著降低的成本达到了甚至超越LLM的准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型推理能力强但服务成本高昂，小语言模型成本低但在难题上可靠性不足。现有混合方案多依赖外部路由器或访问LLM logits，缺乏端到端的成本感知协作机制。

Method: 三阶段训练：控制令牌嵌入学习→卸载导向的监督微调→基于GRPO的成本感知对齐。SLM通过发射控制令牌决定是否向冻结的LLM请求帮助，Collaborate Engine执行单次交接完成补全。

Result: λ=0.05时准确率64.04%（超LLM基线6.36pp），成本降低20.4%；λ=0.6时准确率54.55%，仅1.90%的LLM令牌比例，总成本从49.36美元降至1.78美元。

Conclusion: 学习到的令牌级交接策略能在大幅减少LLM使用的同时保持强推理性能，为成本敏感的LLM部署提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) provide strong reasoning capabilities but are expensive to serve at scale, whereas small language models (SLMs) are cheaper but less reliable on difficult problems. We introduce PyroDash, a cost-aware framework for token-level SLM-LLM collaborative inference. During generation, the SLM decides whether to request assistance by emitting a control token. A Collaborate Engine then sends the query and partial reasoning trace to a frozen LLM for completion through a single handoff. The policy is internalized in the SLM, requiring neither a separate router, LLM retraining, nor access to LLM logits. PyroDash trains the SLM in three stages: control-token embedding learning, offloading-oriented supervised fine-tuning, and cost-aware alignment with Group Relative Policy Optimization. Its reward balances answer accuracy against inference cost normalized by LLM-only inference. Across five mathematical reasoning benchmarks, PyroDash supports different accuracy-cost operating points. With $λ=0.05$, it achieves 64.04 percent average accuracy, 6.36 percentage points above the LLM-only baseline, while reducing cost by 20.4 percent. With $λ=0.6$, it achieves 54.55 percent accuracy with a 1.90 percent LLM token ratio and 0.012 LLM calls per example, reducing total cost from USD 49.36 to USD 1.78. These results show that learned token-level handoffs can reduce LLM use while preserving strong reasoning performance.

</details>


### [115] [Generative AI floods and dilutes the market for books](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20349)
*Tuhin Chakrabarty,Xinyue Liu,Jane C. Ginsburg,Paramveer Dhillon*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 生成式AI可低成本创作长篇小说，虽被视作低质量“残渣”，但通过分析2023-2026年Amazon自出版书籍数据发现，AI含量超25%的书籍虽占销量份额较小，却持续增长并抢占畅销排名，导致市场书籍数量增速远超收入增速，单位书籍收入下降，且AI书籍在语言上更依赖已有作品，这对版权合理使用抗辩具有重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战“AI生成的书籍因质量低劣而不会具有商业影响力”这一普遍假设，实证检验生成式AI对创意市场的实际影响。

Method: 对Amazon上14,419本自出版类型小说进行全文AI检测，匹配至2026年6月的日销售记录，分析AI文本占比>25%的书籍在市场规模、销售份额、排名分布及语言独特性方面的表现。

Result: AI含量高的书籍占目录份额大但销售额份额小，但销售份额随时间增长，并抢占更多前列排名；市场书籍数量增长19.2倍而收入仅增长8.9倍，单位书籍收入下降；无AI文本的书籍在AI扩散高的类型中失去最多市场；畅销AI书籍语言独特性更高且与已有作品的重叠度随收入上升。

Conclusion: 生成式AI通过规模化而非质量重塑创意市场，其商业规模已达到足以影响版权法公平使用抗辩中市场效果考量的程度。

Abstract: Generative AI can produce book-length works of fiction at near-zero cost. These books are often dismissed as low-quality ``slop'' that buyers will ignore, and are assumed to carry little commercial weight. We test that assumption with full-text AI detection across 14,419 self-published genre-fiction books sold on Amazon from 2023 to 2026, matched to daily sales records through June 2026. None of these books disclose whether or not they contain AI-produced content. We find that books for which we detected substantial AI text ($>$ 25\%) make up a large share of the catalog but a smaller share of sales. Even so, they reach commercial scale, winning a growing share of sales over time and taking more of the scarce top-rank positions once held by books with no detected AI text. Over this period, the number of books with observed sales in a quarter grew 19.2-fold, while quarterly revenue grew only 8.9-fold. The market therefore added selling books faster than it added revenue, and revenue per selling book fell across most genres. Books with no AI text lose the most ground in genres with high AI diffusion, and most of all where Kindle Unlimited availability is high. Among top-selling books, those with substantial AI text draw on more distinctive language from existing books than do books with no AI text; for these books overlap rises with revenue, a gradient we do not detect for books with no AI text. Generative AI can thus reshape a creative market through scale rather than quality. Our results bear directly on the market-effect question at the center of the fair use defense to copyright infringement.

</details>


### [116] [Notes to Self: Can LLMs Benefit from Experiential Abstractions?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20372)
*Chang Liu,Xinyu Li,Artur Dubrawski*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型语言模型（LLMs）能否像人类一样，从经验中提取可重复使用的抽象知识（如策略和提醒），并将其存储到可检索的库中。通过从MATH训练集的解题轨迹中提取自然语言抽象，并采用推理时检索或强化学习增强训练提示两种方式，实验表明这些经验抽象能提升LLM在数学和逻辑推理任务上的表现，且自提取抽象与教师提取效果相当，框架可迁移至其他数据集和模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索LLMs是否能够像人类一样，从过往经验中提炼出可复用的抽象知识（如解题策略、注意事项），并利用这些抽象知识持续提升问题解决能力，从而缩小LLMs与人类在经验学习方面的差距。

Method: 从LLMs在MATH训练集上的解题轨迹中，由更强的教师模型或LLMs自身提取自然语言抽象知识，构建可检索的抽象库。然后探索两种使用模式：(1) 推理时从库中检索相关抽象并注入提示；(2) 在强化学习中用抽象增强的训练提示进行训练。

Result: 经验抽象显著提升了LLM在数学和逻辑推理基准上的表现；LLMs自提取的抽象与教师提取的抽象效果相当；该抽象使用框架可迁移至其他数据集和模型。

Conclusion: LLMs能够像人类利用经过提炼的经验一样，提取和应用经验抽象来提升推理能力，表明经验抽象机制在LLM中具有可行性和泛化性。

Abstract: Humans distill experience into reusable abstractions, e.g., strategies and cautionary reminders, and apply them to gradually solve problems more effectively. We study whether Large Language Models (LLMs) can similarly benefit from such experiential abstractions. From LLMs' solution traces on the MATH training set, a stronger teacher or the LLMs themselves extract natural-language abstractions into a retrievable library. We explore two usage modes: (1) inference-time retrieval and (2) reinforcement learning (RL) with abstraction-augmented training prompts. Experiential abstractions improve LLM performance on mathematical and logical reasoning benchmarks. Self-extracted abstractions match teacher-extracted ones, and our abstraction usage framework can transfer to other datasets and models. These findings suggest LLMs can extract and apply experiential abstractions much as humans leverage distilled experience.

</details>


### [117] [LKValues: Aligning Large Language Models with Sri Lankan Societal Values](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20410)
*Nethmi Muthugala,Supryadi,Surangika Ranathunga,Nisansa de Silva,Ruijie Tao,Ovindu Gunatunga,Pengyun Zhu,Shaowei Zhang,Jingting Zheng,Deyi Xiong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出LKValues，首个针对斯里兰卡语（僧伽罗语）的价值观对齐资源套件。通过三语调查获取40项社会价值观，构建了15万条指令语料库LKvaluesIT和1000条评估基准LKvaluesBench。实验表明大型语言模型在低资源文化和价值观对齐上存在差距，而LKValues微调能有效嵌入斯里兰卡价值观。

Method: 1) 对205名受访者进行三语调查，结合全球框架和大模型引导提取本地构念，得到40项多数认同的社会价值观；2) 基于这些价值观构建15万条僧伽罗-英语新闻衍生指令语料库LKvaluesIT；3) 建立1000条评估基准LKvaluesBench；4) 在Qwen3.5-4B-Base、Qwen3.5-9B-Base和Aya-Expanse-8B-Base上微调评测。

Conclusion: LKValues能有效嵌入斯里兰卡价值观，提供了一条可复制的低资源、国家特定多元价值观对齐流程。

Abstract: Value alignment of Large Language Models (LLMs) has been shown to be culturally biased toward Western norms. From a trilingual survey of 205 respondents, blending adapted global frameworks and LLM-elicited local constructs, we derive 40 majority-endorsed societal values. Using these values, we construct LKvaluesIT, a Sinhala-English news-derived instruction corpus containing 150k scenario-based instances, and LKvaluesBench, a value-sensitive evaluation benchmark of 1,000 instances. Our experiments show that newer and larger LLMs still exhibit low-resource and cultural value-alignment gaps. LKValues fine-tuning improves Qwen-family models in English and Sinhala, reducing invalid outputs and cross-lingual disparities, though gains remain model-family dependent. These highlight LKValues efficacy in embedding Sri Lankan values, offering a replicable pipeline for low-resource, country-specific pluralist value alignment. The dataset is publicly available at https://github.com/NextME14/LKValues.

### [118] [SPILLOVER: Measuring Cyberbullying NormPropagation on Social Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19646)
*Arslan Bisharat,Katelyn Skees,Mujtaba Nazari,Ayaan Khan,Manuel Sandoval,Mohammed Abuhamad,Deborah Hall,Yasin Silva*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究社交媒体会话中网络欺凌（CB）在评论间的转移机制，发现前一条CB评论会显著提高下一条评论成为CB的概率，且CB→CB评论对在文本相似度上高于非CB→CB对。研究在多个数据集上验证了结果，并证明“前一条是否为CB”这一单一特征能提升预测性能，可作为实时 moderation 信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多关注网络欺凌的成因和 prevalence，但鲜有研究关注侵略性如何在评论区之间具体传递。理解这种传递机制对设计更好的反欺凌功能具有重要意义。

Method: 使用32,754对连续评论数据（来自430个Instagram会话），采用session固定效应控制、跨会话匹配基线、五种互补的文本相似度方法，并在Reddit、Wikipedia Detox、SOCC三个独立数据集上进行复制验证。

Result: 1) 前一条CB评论显著提高下一条评论成为CB的概率（主要由跨用户传播驱动）；2) CB→CB评论对文本相似度高于NoCB→CB对；3) 非侵略性回复会随着前一条CB严重性增加而变得更负面；4) 这些模式在三个数据集上均得到复制；5) 单一二元特征（前一条是否为CB）能提升预测性能，甚至优于微调后的HateBERT分类器。

Conclusion: 网络欺凌具有评论间传播的链式特征，利用这一简单信号可设计实时 moderation 机制，聚焦于切断传播链而非仅惩罚单个违规者。

Abstract: While certain aspects of cyberbullying (CB) such as its factors and prevalence have been studied extensively, relatively little attention has been given to specifically how the aggression transfers from comment to comment. This understanding could have important implications for designing better anti-bullying features. In this paper, we study multiple aspects of the nature of this aggression transference in social media sessions. Using data from 32,754 consecutive comment pairs from 430 Instagram sessions, we find that a preceding CB comment substantially raises the odds of the next comment being CB, an effect confirmed by session fixed-effects controls and driven primarily by cross-user spread. We also find that $\text{CB} \to \text{CB}$ pairs are more textually similar than $\text{NoCB} \to \text{CB}$ pairs across five complementary methods, and that this pattern holds under a matched cross-session baseline that rules out shared vocabulary, session toxicity, and session length as confounds. Moreover, non-aggressive replies grow more negative as preceding CB severity increases, a graded pattern consistent with automatic emotional influence below the threshold of overt aggression. These key findings replicate across three independent datasets (Reddit, Wikipedia Detox, and SOCC), with spillover rates that track platform visibility design. Finally, we show that a single binary feature (whether the prior comment was CB) improves prediction over session-level baselines and over a fine-tuned HateBERT classifier, serving as a real-time moderation signal that targets the spreading chain rather than individual offenders.

</details>

Result: 识别出9个Stack Overflow主导主题和13个GitHub主题；"How"类型问题占据主导；特定主题（如TFF安装与环境兼容、联邦特征工程与SecureBoost问题）具有高未解决率和长解决时间。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) enables collaborative model training without centralizing raw data, but building and operating FL systems remains difficult due to distributed execution, rapidly evolving frameworks, and privacy and governance requirements. ### [121] [PerfAgent: Profiler-Guided Iterative Refinement for Repository-Level Code Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19653)
*Ryan Deng,Yuanzhe Liu,Bastian Lipka,Yao Ma,Xuhao Chen,Tim Kaler,Jatin Ganhotra*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: PerfAgent是一个由剖析器引导、验证器循环驱动的工作流，通过提供精确的性能反馈，使通用编码智能体在仓库级代码优化任务上的专家级补丁生成率比OpenHands提升一倍以上（GSO上从19.6%到39.2%，SWE-fficiency-Lite上从26%到74%），且成本低于oracle最佳5次采样基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在仓库级代码优化任务上表现不佳，因为仅通过测试不足以保证优化正确性——优化补丁需同时保持行为、提升性能并接近专家级加速。当前智能体常因被抽象层和原生扩展隐藏瓶颈、浅尝辄止或测试不充分而失败。

Method: PerfAgent提出剖析器引导+验证器循环的工作流：1）用性能剖析器定位真实热点而非仅靠运行时间判断；2）将剖析证据作为反馈持续迭代优化；3）验证器在循环中确保补丁保持行为不变性，从而突破浅层优化并避免破坏边界情况。

Result: 在GSO和SWE-fficiency-Lite两个基准上，PerfAgent的专家级补丁生成率分别达到39.2%和74%，相比OpenHands+GPT-5.1的19.6%和26%提升一倍以上，且超越了oracle最佳5次采样基线，同时成本更低。

Conclusion: PerfAgent表明，提供更好的性能反馈（而非更多采样）是提升LLM智能体代码优化能力的关键，其剖析器+验证器循环范式为仓库级性能优化提供了一个有效且经济的解决方案。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents now perform well on correctness-oriented repository-level tasks, including SWE-Bench issue resolution and feature implementation in real codebases. However, they still struggle with repository-level code optimization, which requires preserving behavior while improving runtime performance. Passing tests is not enough in this setting; a patch must preserve behavior, implement code optimization, and approach expert speedups. Current agents often miss bottlenecks hidden behind abstraction layers and native extensions, stop after shallow speedups, or insufficiently test the code patches that thus may silently break edge cases. We present PerfAgent, a profiler-guided, verifier-in-the-loop workflow that gives an off-the-shelf coding agent the feedback needed to find real hotspots, improve beyond the first passing patch, and use profiler evidence rather than timing alone to decide what to optimize next. On two challenging optimization benchmarks, GSO and SWE-fficiency-Lite, PerfAgent more than doubles the rate of expert-matching patches over OpenHands with GPT-5.1, improving from 19.6% to 39.2% on GSO and from 26% to 74% on SWE-fficiency-Lite. It also surpasses an oracle best-of-five baseline at substantially lower cost, showing that the gains come from better feedback rather than additional test-time sampling.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业部署发现LLM生成的单元测试在实际复杂项目中存在编译失败率高、需要昂贵的人工修复、覆盖率提升不稳定等持久问题，研究结果与实用之间存在持续差距。

Method: CATGen采用多阶段设计：结构化上下文检索、确定性测试骨架构建、基于程序分析的后处理。核心思路是用显式工程信息替代LLM对不完备项目上下文的推断，用静态分析替代LLM迭代修复。

Abstract: Automated unit test generation has recently benefited from advances in large language models (LLMs), yet our industrial deployments reveal a persistent gap between promising research results and practical usability. In real-world projects with complex frameworks and cross-file dependencies, LLM-generated tests frequently fail to compile, require costly manual repair, or provide unstable coverage improvements. This paper reports our experience in designing, deploying, and evaluating CATGen, a context-aware workflow for LLM-based unit test generation, informed by repeated industrial failures and refinements. Rather than relying on LLMs to infer incomplete project context, we found that compilation robustness critically depends on making project-level dependencies explicit, stabilizing test class scaffolding, and replacing iterative LLM-based repair with lightweight static analysis. These experience-driven insights shaped CATGen's multi-stage design, which combines structured context retrieval, deterministic test skeleton construction, and program analysis-based post-processing. We evaluate CATGen on real-world complex focal methods from proprietary industrial projects and additionally on the Defects4J benchmark to assess generalizability. Across both settings, CATGen substantially improves compilation success and structural coverage while significantly reducing generation time and token consumption compared to existing LLM-based approaches. Our results demonstrate that reliable LLM-based unit test generation in practice depends less on prompt engineering alone and more on systematic engineering support grounded in real-world development constraints.

### [123] [Bridging Behavior and Implementation: Automated Java Glue Code Generation for Behavior-Driven Development](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19703)
*Xinyu Shi,Zhou Yang,An Ran Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BDD中的胶水代码开发维护劳动密集，需要同时理解行为意图和底层代码。虽然LLM在代码生成方面表现强劲，但将其用于自动胶水代码生成仍未被探索。

Method: 提出AutoGlue层次化多智能体框架，采用行为优先工作流：Behavior Interpreter从场景上下文推导步骤意图，Developer agent检索相关BDD工件和项目代码后生成最终胶水代码。

Result: 在8个开源Java项目的1,307个步骤上评估，相比少样本提示，API F1提升58.7%，CodeBLEU提升43.7%。46.1%的步骤可直接使用，大部分部分正确的输出仅需小幅修改。

Abstract: Behavior-Driven Development (BDD) helps technical and non-technical stakeholders share a common understanding of software requirements through natural-language scenarios. Glue code makes these scenarios executable by mapping each step to the corresponding project code. However, developing and maintaining glue code requires knowledge of both the intended behavior and the underlying codebase, making it a labor-intensive part of BDD as requirements evolve. Although large language models (LLMs) have shown strong code generation capabilities, their use for automated glue code generation remains unexplored. This task requires reasoning over underspecified behavior, related BDD artifacts, and large project codebases. We present AutoGlue, a hierarchical multi-agent framework for automated Java glue code generation. AutoGlue follows a behavior-first workflow that separates behavior interpretation, context retrieval, and code generation. A Behavior Interpreter derives the intent of a step from its scenario context, while a Developer agent retrieves relevant BDD artifacts and project code before generating the final glue code. We evaluate AutoGlue on 1,307 steps from eight open-source Java projects. Compared with few-shot prompting, AutoGlue improves API F1 by 58.7% and CodeBLEU by 43.7%. It produces directly usable glue code for 46.1% of the evaluated steps, while most partially correct outputs require only minor revisions, such as adding missing actions or refining parameters. Ablation results show that behavior interpretation and project-aware context retrieval both contribute substantially to generation quality. These findings demonstrate that LLMs can effectively connect natural-language behavior specifications with project code and support specification-driven software development.

### [124] [Towards Automated Formal Verification of zkEVMs Using LLM-Guided Constraint Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19795)
*Shichen Huang,Zhenghe Jiang,Yi Jiang,Ling-I Wu,Jingyang Li,Guoqiang Li*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: VeriSynth是一个自动化框架，利用LLM将Rust zkEVM操作码代码翻译成Python/Z3验证模型，再由SMT求解器进行形式化验证，在首个源码级zkEVM验证基准上实现了超过90%的bug检测率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: zkEVM实现中的细微bug（如gas计算错误）会导致有效证明认证错误状态，破坏密码学安全保证。现有形式化验证依赖手工规范，效率低下；LLM直接生成规范存在幻觉且缺乏形式化保证。亟需自动化方法将Rust操作码代码转化为可验证的形式化模型。

Method: VeriSynth采用混合范式：LLM仅作为形式化前端，将代码翻译为符号约束；SMT求解器作为正确性仲裁者。核心包含三大组件：语义分解（处理多组件状态转换）、检索增强提示（利用示例引导生成）、验证引导自动修复（闭环迭代修正错误模型）。

Result: 在首个源码级zkEVM验证基准上，VeriSynth的bug检测率超过90%，显著优于直接LLM、对话LLM基线以及生产级手工突变测试套件。消融实验证实每个管道组件对整体效果都至关重要。

Conclusion: VeriSynth证明了LLM+形式化验证的混合范式能有效解决zkEVM代码的自动化形式化验证难题，兼顾了LLM的代码理解能力与SMT求解器的严格正确性保证。

Abstract: Zero-Knowledge Ethereum Virtual Machines (zkEVMs) secure Ethereum rollups by generating zero-knowledge proofs that guarantee off-chain execution correctness. However, subtle implementation bugs (e.g., incorrect gas accounting) can lead to valid proofs certifying semantically faulty states, thereby silently defeating cryptographic guarantees. Formal verification via SMT solvers can prevent this, but is bottlenecked by specification: current zkEVM development practice lacks automated methods to translate Rust opcode handlers into verification models. Current practices rely on unsustainable manual specifications, while LLM-based approaches suffer from hallucination and lack formal guarantees. To address this, we propose VeriSynth, a framework that synthesizes executable Python/Z3 verification models from Rust zkEVM code. VeriSynth enforces a hybrid paradigm: an LLM acts strictly as a formalization frontend to translate code into symbolic constraints, while an SMT solver serves as the correctness arbiter. To handle complex multi-component state transitions, VeriSynth integrates semantic decomposition, retrieval-grounded prompting, and verification-guided auto-repair into a closed-loop pipeline. We evaluate VeriSynth on the first source-level zkEVM verification benchmark, encompassing both correct and faulty opcode implementations. VeriSynth achieves a bug detection rate of over 90%, substantially outperforming direct and conversational LLM baselines, as well as a production-grade handwritten mutation-testing suite. Ablation studies confirm that each pipeline component is critical to the framework's overall effectiveness.

</details>


### [125] [Beyond Fail-to-Pass: Iterative Hardening of Co-Generated Bug Reproduction Tests and Fixes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19843)
*Yuhao Tan,Zhibang Yang,Fangkai Yang,Yuan Yao,Yu Kang,Lu Wang,Pu Zhao,Xin Zhang,Xiaoxing Ma,Qingwei Lin,Saravan Rajmohan,Dongmei Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出CoHarden框架，通过区分"严格"与"宽松"的bug复现测试(BRT)，并引入"宽松信号"作为循环收敛标准，迭代强化测试与补丁以抵御突变补丁，在SWE-bench Verified上达到69.4%的修复率，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有APR中，BRT的评估仅依赖fail-to-pass (F->P)标准，但该标准不足以确保下游修复成功——部分F->P BRT虽能复现症状，却仍容许看似正确实则错误的补丁通过，即存在"宽松"BRT问题。此外，协同生成（cogeneration）会导致测试-修复错误耦合，使得F->P检查在两者都错误时仍可能通过。需要一种更严格的BRT质量度量与生成方法。

Method: 1) 形式化定义"严格"与"宽松"BRT，将F->P BRT进一步细分；2) 提出CoHarden框架：先生成测试，再迭代强化测试与补丁，以"宽松信号"（Lax signal）作为循环收敛标准，直至生成的测试不再容许宽松回归（即无法通过错误补丁的验证）；3) 使用突变补丁（surviving mutation patches）作为对抗样本进行迭代硬化。

Result: 在SWE-bench Verified上，CoHarden达到69.4% Resolved和78.9% F->P，比最强fix-only基线高+9.6个百分点，比最强cogeneration基线高+7.9个百分点。增益在多个LLM骨干网络和基准测试上保持一致。

Conclusion: F->P标准不足以评估BRT质量，需区分严格与宽松BRT；协同生成中的测试-修复错误耦合是实际隐患；CoHarden通过迭代硬化有效缓解上述问题，显著提升APR修复成功率。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have made automated program repair (APR) increasingly practical for real-world bugs, but repairing directly from bug reports remains underconstrained. Bug reproduction tests (BRTs) help close this gap by turning a bug report into an executable, bug-specific signal that can guide repair and validate candidate patches. Existing work has therefore studied BRT generation as a core subproblem in APR and mainly evaluates a generated BRT using the fail-to-pass (F->P) criterion, which requires the test to fail on the buggy code but pass on the golden fix. We show that F->P alone is insufficient when the goal of a BRT is to improve downstream repair. In particular, some F->P BRTs are lax, reproducing the observed symptom yet still admitting plausible-but-incorrect patches. We formalize this missing quality dimension by separating F->P BRTs into rigorous and lax ones, and show empirically that only the former consistently improve repair success. We further find that co-generation introduces test--fix error coupling, where the in-trajectory fail-to-pass (F->P) check can pass even when both the generated patch and generated test are wrong. Based on these findings, we propose CoHarden, a co-generation framework that uses the Lax signal as an in-loop convergence criterion. CoHarden first generates a test before any fix, then iteratively hardens the test and fix against surviving mutation patches until the generated test no longer admits Lax regressions. Experiments show that CoHarden reaches 69.4% Resolved and 78.9% F->P on SWE-bench Verified, outperforming the strongest fix-only and cogeneration baselines by +9.6 and +7.9 percentage points in Resolved, respectively, with consistent gains across LLM backbones and benchmarks.

</details>


### [126] [Towards Reliable C-to-Rust Translation with Rule-Guided Reasoning and Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19966)
*Feng Luo,Jiachen Liu,Cuiyun Gao,Jia Feng,Kui Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出TRAVEL框架，通过规则引导的蒙特卡洛树搜索推理路径构建和强化学习相结合，解决LLM在C代码转Rust时对Rust语法规则理解不足和语义捕获不准确的问题，在多个基准测试上显著提升了翻译正确性和编译成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将遗留C程序迁移到Rust是提升软件内存安全性的重要方向，但人工重写成本高昂。LLM自动化翻译存在两个关键问题：(1) LLM对Rust特定规则识别能力有限，常产生语法错误的翻译；(2) LLM难以准确捕获复杂代码的语义，导致语义错误的翻译。

Method: TRAVEL框架包含两个模块：(1) 基于蒙特卡洛树搜索(MCTS)的推理路径构建模块，由Rust特定规则引导搜索方向，使翻译步骤符合LLM常违反的语法规则；(2) 强化学习模块，将执行反馈与推理质量信号相结合，鼓励模型构建能准确捕获程序语义的推理路径，确保生成的Rust代码保留原始C程序的预期行为。

Result: 在xCodeEval基准上，TRAVEL在所有三个骨干LLM上优于所有基线方法，相比最强提示基线IRENE，计算准确率提升26.22%，编译成功率提升18.77%。在HW-Bench和OS-Bench上，编译成功率分别提升18.28%和16.51%，不安全率分别降低13.06%和13.08%。

Conclusion: TRAVEL通过规则引导推理与强化学习的结合，有效解决了LLM在C-to-Rust翻译中的语法和语义问题，显著提升了翻译质量和安全性，在公共基准、Linux内核和工业数据集上均表现优异。

Abstract: The migration of legacy C programs to Rust has become an important direction for improving software memory safety while alleviating the high cost of manual rewriting. Leveraging large language models (LLMs) for automated C-to-Rust translation has emerged as a promising direction. However, existing LLM-based approaches remain limited. On the one hand, LLMs exhibit limited capability in identifying Rust-specific rules, and inadequate handling of Rust syntax often results in incorrect translations. On the other hand, existing LLMs often struggle to accurately capture the semantics of complex code, resulting in incorrect translations. To address these challenges, we propose a Translation fRAmework Via rule-guided reasoning and rEinforcement Learning, namely TRAVEL, consisting of two modules. The first module employs Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS)-based reasoning path construction guided by Rust-specific rules, steering the search toward translation steps that respect the syntactic rules that LLMs frequently violate. The second module introduces reinforcement learning that couples execution feedback with reasoning-quality signals, encouraging the model to construct reasoning paths that accurately capture program semantics, thereby ensuring that the generated Rust code preserves the intended behavior of the original C program. We evaluate TRAVEL on three datasets: xCodeEval (a public benchmark), OS-Bench (functions collected from the Linux kernel), and HW-Bench (an industrial dataset from Huawei). On xCodeEval, TRAVEL outperforms all baselines across three backbone LLMs. In particular, compared to the strongest prompting baseline IRENE, TRAVEL improves computational accuracy (CA) by 26.22% and compilation success rate (CSR) by 18.77%. On HW-Bench and OS-Bench, TRAVEL further improves CSR by 18.28% and 16.51%, respectively, while reducing unsafe rate (UR) by 13.06% and 13.08%, respectively.

</details>


### [127] [SequenceFI: Non-intrusive Temporal Fault Injection for Microservice Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20050)
*Yuzhen Tan,Jian Wang,Bing Li,Shaolin Tan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出SequenceFI，一种非侵入式的时序故障注入框架，通过观察消息事件、传播时间证据、触发时序保护条件，实现对微服务系统中时间敏感故障的精确复现，相比基线方法减少95.91%的端到端搜索时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有请求级故障注入技术虽能控制故障的位置和类型，但无法控制故障在分布式执行中的激活时机，导致难以复现时序相关的故障（如状态变更后的失败、顺序敏感并发响应、下游重复调用的部分失败）。

Method: SequenceFI通过观察消息级发送和接收事件，沿请求执行传播紧凑的时间证据，仅在满足时间保护条件时触发故障；从轨迹中合成时间保护条件，减少穷举搜索需求，无需修改应用代码或序列化库。

Result: 在Kubernetes上实现，基于四个微服务基准测试、九种时序故障场景和450次有效试验中，达到100%的时序成功（无提前或多次注入），平均一次尝试找到有效配置，端到端搜索时间减少95.91%。

Conclusion: SequenceFI能够高效、精确地复现微服务系统中的时序相关故障，大幅减少搜索开销，为非侵入式时序故障注入提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Fault injection is widely used to evaluate the resilience of microservice systems, where client requests often span multiple services and execution stages. Existing request-level techniques usually control where and what faults are injected, but not when they are activated within a distributed execution. This limitation makes it difficult to reproduce timing-dependent failures, such as failures after state-changing side effects, order-sensitive concurrent responses, and partial failures among repeated downstream calls. This paper presents SequenceFI, a non-intrusive framework for temporal fault injection in microservice systems. SequenceFI observes message-level send and receive events, propagates compact temporal evidence along request executions, and triggers faults only when occurrence-sensitive temporal guards are satisfied. It further synthesizes temporal guards from traces, reducing the need for exhaustive enumeration of temporal fault-injection configurations, while requiring no modifications to application code or serialization libraries. We implement SequenceFI on Kubernetes and evaluate it on four widely used microservice benchmarks. Across nine temporal-fault scenarios and 450 valid trials, SequenceFI achieves 100.0\% temporal success without premature or multiple injections, finds effective configurations in one attempt on average, and reduces aggregate end-to-end search time by 95.91\% compared with H-Random.

</details>


### [128] [Multi-stage Dynamic Selection for Cross-Project Defect Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20151)
*Juscimara G. Avelino,Juscelino S. A. Junior,George D. C. Cavalcanti,Rafael M. O. Cruz*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向跨项目缺陷预测的两阶段多分类器集成选择框架，先在项目级筛选能覆盖多个训练项目的分类器组合，再在测试时针对目标项目每个模块动态选择最合适的分类器，从而缓解分布偏移问题，在82个项目上超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统跨项目缺陷预测因训练项目与目标项目之间存在分布偏移，导致模型性能下降。现有方法对整个目标项目使用同一组分类器，无法适应不同模块的差异特性。

Method: 提出两阶段多分类器系统选择方案：第一阶段在项目级评估多种MCS配置，选择覆盖广、泛化好的分类器组合，确保分类器多样性；第二阶段在测试时为每个新模块选择最擅长的分类器进行预测，实现模块级模型选择。

Result: 在82个项目、4个基准数据集上的实验表明，所提方法在大多数场景下优于当前最优的CPDP方法。

Conclusion: 模块级的动态分类器选择能更鲁棒地应对训练与目标项目间的分布变化，有效提升跨项目缺陷预测性能，代码已开源。

Abstract: Cross-Project Defect Prediction (CPDP) involves building models using data from external projects, called training projects, to predict modules from the target project. However, traditional CPDP methods suffer from the distribution shift between training and target projects that affects the model's performance. This paper proposes a novel CPDP framework that addresses this issue by proposing a two-stage multiple classifier system (MCS) selection scheme: one working at the project level and another at the module level. In the first stage, the framework evaluates multiple possible MCS configurations to find one that covers and generalizes well across multiple training projects. Consequently, the proposal is likely to obtain a diverse set of classifiers, each specialized in tackling software modules with distinct characteristics. The second selection stage operates at test time, selecting the most competent classifiers to predict each new module in the target project. Unlike previous approaches that apply the same classifiers to the entire target project, the proposed framework performs module-level model selection. This way, the system is more robust to changes in distributions between training and target projects because the selected set of classifiers is module-dependent. Our experimental results using 82 projects from four different CPDP benchmark datasets demonstrate that the proposed approach outperforms the state-of-the-art CPDP methods in most scenarios. The code, dataset, and further details about the proposed method are publicly available at https://github.com/jsaj/Multi_DES.

### [129] [How Developers Use Relation Chains in Gerrit-Based Review Ecosystems: An Empirical Study Across Three Open-Source Ecosystems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20189)
*Ahmed Belhouchette,Moataz Chouchen,Marouene Chaieb,Mohammad Hamdaqa Abdelwahab Hamou-Lhadj*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究分析了Gerrit生态系统中29,580条关系链(涉及401,256个变更),发现链式依赖在15个项目的14个中愈发普遍,链式变更合并时间比同等大小的独立变更慢2.6倍,审查活动在上下游间显著相关(ρ=0.43-0.61),33.5%的链成员在审查中发生结构性演变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发者越来越多地通过提交一系列相关变更而非单一庞大的变更来协调依赖性的审查工作流,形成"关系链"这一结构化审查单元。然而,这些依赖结构如何影响审查动态和结果尚未被充分理解。

Method: 从15个仓库(OpenStack、Wikimedia、ONAP三大Gerrit生态系统)收集29,580条关系链(401,256个变更),使用Mann-Kendall趋势检验、Mann-Whitney检验(Cliff's delta)、Spearman相关性分析等方法进行定量分析。

Result: 链式变更占比5%-49%,在14/15的项目中呈上升趋势;链式变更合并耗时中位数是同等规模独立变更的2.6倍,且差距在大变更中进一步扩大;基础变更与衍生变更的审查活动共变(ρ=0.43-0.61,14-15/15项目);33.5%的链成员在审查中发生结构演变。

Conclusion: 关系链作为具有内部结构的持久协调单元运行,传统的变更中心分析无法捕捉其特性。未来的审查分析、审阅者分配系统和AI辅助审查工具应基于链而非孤立变更进行推理。

Abstract: Background. Developers increasingly coordinate dependent review workflows by submitting sequences of related changes rather than monolithic ones. In Gerrit, these dependencies form relation chains: structured review units that link changes together. As chains become more common, they shape review activities through synchronization overhead, CI amplification, and merge-ordering constraints.
  Aim. We investigate how developers adopt relation chains and how these dependency structures influence review dynamics and outcomes.
  Method. We analyze 29,580 relation chains from 15 repositories across three Gerrit ecosystems (OpenStack, Wikimedia, and ONAP), comprising 401,256 changes, using Mann-Kendall trend tests, Mann-Whitney tests with Cliff's delta for chain-vs-solo comparisons, and Spearman correlations for base-descendant dependencies.
  Results. Chain prevalence ranges from 5% to 49% across projects, increasing in 14 of 15. Chain changes take a median of 2.6 times longer to merge than size-matched solo changes, with the gap widening for very large changes. Review effort propagates through dependency-linked review workflows: base-change review activity co-varies with descendant review activity (rho = 0.43-0.61 in 14-15 of 15 projects), and 33.5% of chain members undergo structural evolution during review.
  Conclusions. Relation chains operate as durable, ecosystem-shaped coordination units with internal structure that change-centric analyses cannot capture. Future review analytics, reviewer-assignment systems, and AI-assisted review tools should reason over chains rather than isolated changes.

### [130] [Don't Trust the Label: License Laundering in AI Supply Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20300)
*James Jewitt,Hao Li,Gopi Krishnan Rajbahadur,Bram Adams,Ahmed E. Hassan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 这篇论文追踪了Hugging Face和GitHub上23万多个数据集→模型→应用链条，发现62.3%的链条中至少有一个无许可证声明的人工制品，且具有义务性许可证（如GPL）的端到端存活率不足7%，而宽松许可证存活率高达95.1%，揭示了AI供应链中普遍的"许可证洗白"现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI制品在多平台供应链中流转，许可证义务本应随再分发传播，但尚无人实证测量这些义务是否在链条中得以保留，还是被剥离或替换。

Method: 追踪232,270条数据集→模型→应用链条，量化两种许可证洗白形式：(1)无许可证声明时下游获得标签；(2)一个许可证类别被另一个替换。分析端到端许可证存活率。

Result: 62.3%的链条经过至少一个无许可证声明的人工制品（集中在少量基础数据集）；所有义务性许可证类别端到端存活率低于7%，而宽松类别达95.1%。

Conclusion: AI供应链中存在严重的许可证义务流失问题，论文为从业者、模型发布者、权利人和平台所有者提供了可操作的建议。

Abstract: AI artifacts move through a multi-platform supply chain, spanning datasets and models on Hugging Face and applications on GitHub. While each artifact carries a license whose obligations should propagate through redistribution, no study has yet measured whether those obligations survive the chain or are stripped and replaced as artifacts move downstream. We trace 232,270 dataset$\rightarrow$model$\rightarrow$application chains and quantify two forms of license laundering: when artifacts with no declared license acquire definitive labels downstream, and when one declared license category replaces another during redistribution. We find that 62.3% of chains pass through at least one artifact with no declared license (concentrated in a small set of foundational datasets), and that every obligation-bearing license category falls below 7% end-to-end survival while the Permissive category reaches 95.1%. Based on these findings, we provide actionable recommendations for practitioners, model publishers, rights holders, and platform owners.

### [131] [Multi-Source and Cross-Scenario Strategy-Guided Code Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20353)
*Yuwei Zhao,Qianyu Xiao,Ye Cui,Yijun Yu,Yingfei Xiong*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出MoST框架，通过跨知识源和跨场景的策略整合，显著提升LLM代码优化的效果，在多种编程语言的基准测试和实际项目中超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的代码优化方法只能从历史提交中提取策略，无法利用教科书、网页等其他知识源；且策略只能应用于来源场景，无法跨语言迁移。亟需解决这两个限制。

Method: MoST将不同知识源的信息统一表示为证据对象，通过自平衡加权聚类算法进行跨源跨场景聚类以识别策略，并通过示例迁移过程将策略转移到目标场景，生成静态分析规则指导LLM优化。

Result: 在151个C/C++、150个Python、50个Rust优化任务上，与SemOpt相比生成的精确匹配补丁多24.44%-180.00%，语义等价补丁多21.88%-37.50%；在15个真实项目中性能提升19.72%-717.42%。

Conclusion: MoST通过多源知识整合和跨场景迁移，有效提升了代码优化效果，显著优于现有方法。

Abstract: Automated code optimization improves program performance by refactoring source code, and recent studies use LLMs to generate optimization patches. The newest approaches are strategy-guided: they summarize strategies from historical optimization commits as static analysis rules, and use these rules to match code locations for LLMs to optimize. However, these approaches have two limitations: (1) the strategies may come from other knowledge sources, such as textbooks and web pages, but the existing approaches cannot utilize them; (2) a strategy may be applicable to different scenarios, e.g., different programming languages, but existing approaches can only formalize strategies for the scenario to which the source commit belongs. To address these limitations, we propose MoST, an LLM-based code optimization framework that integrates multiple knowledge sources across scenarios. MoST uniformly represents items in different knowledge sources as evidence objects, clusters them in a cross-source and cross-scenario manner to identify strategies, and transfers them to the target scenario when necessary for generating static analysis rules. To implement this process, MoST employs a novel self-balanced weighted clustering algorithm to balance evidence objects from different knowledge sources, and a novel example transfer procedure to ensure the quality of the generated rules when transferring across scenarios. On a benchmark containing 151 C/C++, 150 Python, and 50 Rust historical optimization tasks, compared with SemOpt, MoST yields 24.44%-180.00% and 21.88%-37.50% more patches that are exactly the same as or semantically equivalent to developer patches, respectively. When optimizing 15 real-world projects, MoST achieves 19.72%-717.42% maximum improvements and 4.44%-258.17% average improvements for the performance tests in the projects, significantly outperforming SemOpt and Codex.

</details>


### [132] [The ICSE 2026 Shadow PC: Training the Next Generation of Reviewers Through Deliberate Practice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20396)
*Christian Kästner,Michael Hilton,Jonathan Bell,Francisco Gomes de Oliveira Neto*

With 102 participants completing the program and reviewing 117 papers, 97% recommending the experience, and positive reception from authors (67% finding reviews helpful), the program demonstrates that rigorous reviewer training is achievable at scale. We share lessons learned and propose shadow PC area chairs as a mechanism for sustainable scaling and leadership development.

### [133] [FineServe: A Fine-Grained Dataset and Characterization of Global LLM Serving Workloads](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19349)
*Tiancheng Zhang,Shaoyuan Huang,Mingyuan Wang,Yunfeng Zhao,Xiaofei Wang,Wenyu Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FineServe是一个从全球商业平台收集的多模型LLM服务负载数据集，揭示了不同模型架构、规模和任务意图下的真实服务动态与波动规律，并提供了可配置的工作负载生成器，用于评估多模型服务系统中的路由、调度和容量规划策略。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as always-on online services, making efficient LLM serving a critical systems challenge. Method: OpenEvoShield包含四个模块：M1非对称速率控制器解耦攻击侧与正常侧的更新速率；M2正常边界更新器以慢速率维护动态行为边界；M3 EWC正则化策略集成实现快速适应同时避免灾难性遗忘；M4能量基多粒度检测器融合节点、子图和图级证据，将新型攻击分类为分布外样本。

Existing defenses treat deployment as a closed-world problem and degrade rapidly once either distribution shifts beyond training coverage. We propose OpenEvoShield, a co-evolutionary continual defense framework for LLM-MAS. An asymmetric rate controller (M1) decouples fast attack-side and slow normal-side learning rates from dual drift signals. A normal-boundary updater (M2) maintains a dynamic behavioral boundary at the slow rate, while an EWC-regularized policy ensemble (M3) fast-adapts without catastrophic forgetting. ### [137] [FormulaSPIN: Self-Play Fine-Tuning for Natural Language to Spreadsheet Formula Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19354)
*Cy Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出FORMULASPIN框架，通过自对弈机制突破公式生成任务中监督微调的性能天花板，无需额外数据即达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子表格公式编写对用户存在巨大障碍，现有方法依赖静态监督数据，在标注有限时性能迅速饱和。

Method: FORMULASPIN框架：1) 利用公式的可执行性作为隐式监督信号，区分语义错误与有效风格变体；2) 将训练建模为双人博弈，主模型学习偏好真实公式而非旧版本生成的公式，执行反馈按粒度排序输出，实现从语义正确性到风格优化的自适应课程；3) ExecVote投票机制处理多种有效公式。

Result: NL2FORMULA上达到74.9%精确匹配和87.1%执行准确率，超越传统SFT和前沿闭源模型，性能与使用额外偏好标注的模型相当。

Conclusion: 自对弈在低资源任务中具有巨大潜力，且该方法可扩展至其他可执行领域。

Abstract: Spreadsheet applications are used by hundreds of millions worldwide, yet writing formulas remains a significant barrier. Existing approaches rely on static supervised data, which quickly saturates on limited annotations. In this paper, we introduce FORMULASPIN, a self-play framework that breaks the ceiling of supervised fine-tuning by enabling iterative self-improvement without any additional data. Vanilla SPIN fails on this task: it uniformly penalizes every non-matching output, so execution-equivalent alternatives are punished as negatives in one example while serving as ground truth in another, producing contradictory gradients. Our framework resolves this by exploiting formula generation's unique advantage: binary executability provides implicit supervision that separates semantic errors from valid stylistic variants. We frame training as a two-player game in which the main player learns to prefer ground-truth formulas over those from its previous version, while execution feedback sorts outputs into distinct granularities-enabling an adaptive curriculum that shifts from semantic correctness to stylistic refinement. To further increase accuracy, we incorporate ExecVote, a semantic-level voting mechanism that naturally handles multiple valid formulations. Experiments on multiple benchmarks demonstrate that FORMULASPIN achieves state-of-the-art performance, with 74.9% exact match and 87.1% execution accuracy on NL2FORMULA, matching models trained with additional preference annotations while outperforming both traditional SFT and frontier proprietary models. These findings underscore self-play's potential to tackle scarce data tasks and open the door to extending it beyond executable domains.

### [138] [Information Discernment in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19355)
*Joshua Ashkinaze,Laura Kurek,Alina Faisal,Tongyuan Miao,Mariam Joseph,Ceren Budak,Eric Gilbert*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出信息辨别（Information Discernment）概念，并构建Learn2Discern（L2D）框架与基准测试。通过13个模型、近67万次试验发现，LLMs在来源辨别和真相辨别上均接近随机水平，更依赖来源流行度而非可靠性，且无论信息是否改善其立场都几乎同样更新。新模型和大型模型改善了真相辨别，但来源辨别仍是盲点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLMs越来越多地使用外部知识源（如互联网），但它们是否能够恰当评估信息来源的可靠性（来源辨别）以及信息是否使自身更接近真相（真相辨别）？这一问题尚未被系统形式化和评估。

Method: 形式化定义了信息辨别（Information Discernment），提出Learn2Discern（L2D）实验框架，基于三条规范公理构建可解释指标。进行预注册、配额匹配的用户研究（n=299）验证公理的外部有效性。在13个模型、近67万次试验上进行评估，并设计推理时干预方法。

Result: 模型在来源辨别和真相辨别上均接近随机水平；模型对来源流行度的依赖是可靠性的两倍；模型在信息改善或恶化其立场时的更新幅度几乎相同；模型在自身先验已最准确的数据集上整合外部知识最有效；新模型和大型模型改善了真相辨别但未改善来源辨别。

Conclusion: LLMs在信息辨别上存在系统性的双重失败，来源辨别是当前模型复杂化无法解决的盲点。但简单的推理时干预可同时改善两种辨别能力。随着LLMs取代传统搜索，这一问题的重要性将日益增长。

Abstract: LLMs are increasingly used with external knowledge sources like the internet. Do they weigh information appropriately -- updating more for reliable sources (source discernment) and more when claims bring priors closer to the truth (truth discernment)? We formalize this as information discernment and introduce Learn2Discern (L2D), an experimental framework and benchmark grounded in three normative axioms with interpretable metrics. To establish external validity, a pre-registered, quota-matched user study (n=299) confirms that real LLM users endorse all three axioms and report that violations reduce their trust and usage intent. Across 13 models and nearly 670K trials, we find consistent failures across both dimensions: models perform near chance on source and truth discernment, rely on source popularity twice as much as source reliability, and update roughly equally whether a claim improves or worsens their position relative to the ground truth. Models integrate external knowledge most effectively on datasets where their priors are already the most accurate. Newer and larger models improve truth discernment but not source discernment, a blind spot that model complexity does not address. We identify simple inference-time interventions that improve both forms of discernment. We release our dataset and survey as a testbed for a core alignment property that scales in importance as LLMs replace traditional search.

NEXUS combines deterministic safety rules, argument-level inspection, and a calibrated logistic-regression risk score for graded escalation. On a 128-instance synthetic benchmark, NEXUS achieves an F1 score of 0.949 and a 4-class intervention accuracy of 0.6406, outperforming rule-only intervention selection by 27.3 percentage points. On the rule-blind NEXUS-Stress benchmark, NEXUS reaches an F1 score of 0.881, highlighting the difficulty of fine-grained intervention routing. With 0.205 ms median latency, NEXUS adds under 0.1% overhead to typical agent loops. Code, benchmarks, and the calibrated risk scorer are publicly released.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Recent advances in recommender systems (RS) have shown substantial performance gains through generative modelling. In practice, recommendation often involves constructing slates -- ordered lists of items -- that must satisfy multiple objectives beyond relevance, such as constraints defined over item attributes or fairness constraints. Existing multiobjective approaches either rely on post-processing techniques designed for non-generative settings, or incorporate auxiliary objectives directly into model training. The former does not explicitly account for the sequential nature of generative RS, while the latter is often impractical in large-scale systems.
  We propose a lightweight, inference-time decoding layer that augments autoregressive generative RS to support multiobjective slate generation without modifying or retraining the underlying model. We formulate decoding as an online constrained optimisation problem, where items are selected sequentially, and trade-offs between relevance and auxiliary objectives are adjusted dynamically based on the remaining constraint slack, i.e., how much of each objective remains to be satisfied. This is implemented via a stochastic primal-dual approximation scheme that balances relevance and auxiliary objectives during generation.
  We provide theoretical guarantees on constraint violation and regret, and evaluate the proposed approach through extensive offline experiments and a large-scale online A/B experiment in a real-world recommender system. Our results show consistent improvements in multiobjective trade-offs, including a +1.8\% gain in the auxiliary objectives achieved at zero cost to user satisfaction.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长链式推理模型（如DeepSeek-R1）的推理上下文越来越长，标准自注意力的O(n²)计算复杂度导致推理成本急剧上升，限制了长CoT推理在实际生产环境中的部署。

Method: LISA是即插即用的注意力替换模块，包含两个并行组件：(1) 线性注意力模块（O(n)复杂度）提供长程记忆；(2) 闪电索引器选择Top-M重要Token送入稀疏自注意力。两分支通过门控机制融合。两阶段训练：阶段1用知识蒸馏初始化线性注意力+滑动窗口注意力；阶段2引入索引器替代滑动窗口，通过逐头KL散度损失对齐教师模型注意力模式。

Result: 在DeepSeek-distilled-Qwen模型上，16K上下文下实现50%推理加速，在AIME和MATH-500等推理基准上平均性能提升5.6%。

Conclusion: LISA通过线性注意力与稀疏注意力的混合设计，有效解决了长序列推理中的计算瓶颈，无需从头预训练即可部署，在加速推理的同时提升了推理性能。

Abstract: Recent advances in long chain-of-thought reasoning models such as DeepSeek-R1 have led to increasingly longer inference context lengths under the test-time scaling paradigm. However, the O(n^2) computational complexity of standard self-attention causes inference costs to grow sharply with long sequences, limiting the deployment of long-CoT reasoning in production settings. To address this, we propose LISA (Linear-Indexed Sparse Attention), a plug-and-play attention replacement module that requires no pretraining from scratch. LISA integrates two lightweight components in parallel within the original model: (1) a Linear Attention module that provides long-range memory with O(n) time complexity; (2) a Lightning Indexer that selects the top-M important tokens from the full context to feed into a Sparse Self-Attention. The two branches are fused via a gating mechanism, reducing inference complexity from O(n^2) to O(nM) (M << n) for generating n tokens. We design a two-stage training pipeline: Stage 1 initializes the model by integrating the linear attention to capture long-range dependencies, complemented by a sliding-window attention mechanism that is optimized via knowledge distillation to approximate the full self-attention distribution of a frozen teacher model. In Stage 2, we further introduce the Indexer to replace the static sliding-window mechanism, enabling dynamic token selection from broader contexts. The Indexer is trained using a novel per-head KL divergence loss, which aligns its selection behavior with the attention patterns of the teacher model. Experiments on DeepSeek-distilled-Qwen models demonstrate that LISA achieves a 50% inference speedup under 16K-token context, while improving average performance by 5.6% on reasoning benchmarks including AIME and MATH-500.

*Shengtong Zhu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 提出的MemHop基准和ProGraph架构有效填补了多跳记忆评估与实现的空白，不同组件具有明确的机制专业化分工，且整体性能优于现有方法。

Abstract: Long-term memory is essential for LLM agents that interact across sessions, yet current memory benchmarks primarily evaluate single-hop recall, leaving multi-hop association largely unmeasured. Second, we present Profile-Graph Memory (ProGraph), a two-layer memory architecture combining (i) profile expansion -- substring-matched traversal of entity names that naturally appear in LLM-written profile narratives, a minimal alternative to explicit knowledge-graph construction -- and (ii) compression residuals -- exact dates, quantities, and named items co-extracted with each profile update at zero extra API cost. Third, a full-grid ablation shows cross-benchmark mechanism specialization: profile expansion drives multi-hop reasoning (-22.6pp on MemHop when removed) while compression residuals drive precision recall (-8.6pp on LoCoMo when not co-extracted), with cross-effects under 3pp within a single architecture. ProGraph averages 80.1% on MemHop (matching the FullContext reference) and 78.4% on LoCoMo (exceeding FullContext by 11.3pp), outperforming Mem0, A-Mem, HippoRAG, and RAG on both. We release MemHop, ProGraph, and baseline implementations.

This view frames lifting as an efficient use of symmetry across instances, and shattering as the refinement of coarse lifted structures into more specific subtypes. The resulting steering direction is constructed as a Cohen's-$d$-weighted combination of SAE decoder rows, providing an optimization-free direction motivated by Fisher-LDA under approximate SAE-feature decorrelation. Across three Gemma-family models, four behavioral domains, and 356 layer-strength configurations, the method produces measurable domain-specific shifts while revealing a substantial gap between raw attribute movement and quality-preserving generation. ### [150] [Spectral-LSH: Sub-Quadratic Prompt Compression via Krylov-Projected Locality-Sensitive Hashing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19368)
*Ali Mahdavi,Azaseh Zamanifar,Amirfarhad Farhadi,Omid Kashefi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Spectral-LSH，一种无需训练的长文本提示压缩方法，利用Krylov子空间和随机特征近似注意力核算子，在注意力特征空间中对相似Token进行SimHash聚合，在16倍压缩率下显著优于分块方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长文本推理中，预填充阶段的注意力机制与序列长度呈二次方关系，导致计算开销过大。现有方法需要训练或显式构造注意力核矩阵，效率低下。

Method: 1) 使用Krylov子空间方法结合随机特征，近似注意力核算子的主导成分，避免O(N²)显式计算；2) 在注意力特征空间中应用SimHash对相似Token进行分组；3) 将分组后的Token聚合为宏Token，并赋予因果位置分配；4) 自适应后端在低压缩率下使用分块路径，高压缩率下使用谱聚类路径。

Result: 在C4数据集上评估Mistral-7B-Instruct-v0.3等模型。4倍压缩率以下，轻量级分块最优；8倍以上，谱方法优于分块。16倍压缩率下，Qwen2.5-7B将PPL比值从353.409降至196.963，Qwen2.5-14B从9.533降至3.427。在结构化压力测试中，局部LSH在8倍压缩率下全面优于分块。

Conclusion: Spectral-LSH提供了一种无需训练、高效的长文本提示压缩方案，存在压缩率相变现象，自适应后端能兼顾不同压缩率下的质量与延迟需求。

Abstract: Long-prompt inference remains expensive because prefill attention scales quadratically with sequence length. We propose Spectral-LSH, a training-free prompt compression method that operates before the prompt enters the language model. Spectral-LSH approximates the dominant components of an implicit attention-kernel operator using a Krylov subspace method together with random features, avoiding explicit $O(N^2)$ attention-kernel materialization. It then applies SimHash in the resulting attention eigenspace to group similar tokens and aggregate them into macro-tokens with causal positional assignments.
  We evaluate Mistral-7B-Instruct-v0.3, Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct, and Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct on C4. Our experiments reveal a compression-ratio phase transition. Below $ρ= 4 \times$, local token redundancy is low enough that lightweight chunking typically provides the best latency--quality trade-off. Above $ρ= 8 \times$, the spectral path preserves quality that chunking loses. At $ρ= 16 \times$, Qwen2.5-7B (adaptive) reduces the PPL ratio from 353.409 to 196.963, while Qwen2.5-14B (adaptive) reduces it from 9.533 to 3.427.
  On a small long-context structured stress test containing JSON-like, code-like, and table-like inputs, local LSH also improves every metric over chunking at $8 \times$. The adaptive backend captures both regimes by using the chunk path at low compression and spectral clustering at high compression, although chunking remains the fastest backend in total latency.

</details>


### [151] [Beyond Tracking or Shortcut: Composition-Bounded Predictive States in Poker Autoregressive Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19369)
*Quanhao Li,Qianyu Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究不完美信息博弈（Limit Hold'em）中，自回归模型的隐状态是否真的维持了对手牌的后验信念分布。结果表明，虽然隐状态能预测对手范围和行动，但大部分信息来自可见的公开下注组合，而非残差隐状态结构，作者称之为"组合约束的预测支持"。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 隐状态探针常能恢复潜在标签，但这并不足以证明模型维持了后验信念分布。作者希望厘清这种歧义性，检验模型隐状态是否真正编码了对手牌的后验信念。

Method: 在无范围限制的Limit Hold'em自回归模型上（仅用行动和价值目标训练），进行对手范围探针实验，并通过动作/价值控制、公开下注组合基线、残差隐状态探针、以及合成控制与oracle验证等多种对比分析。

Result: 1. 三颗种子中有两颗对手范围探针为正；2. 行为头预测留出行动比基线高约5个百分点；3. 公开下注组合解释的对手范围信号多于残差隐状态；4. 组合+残差隐状态探针准确率远低于纯组合基线；5. 匹配组合比较在所有种子中均为负。

Conclusion: 存在"组合约束的预测支持"模式：隐状态虽与行为和对手范围相关，但可恢复的范围信息主要来自可见下注组合，而非残差隐状态结构。因此，积极的信念探针结果在作为信念追踪的证据之前，应通过针对性替代假设进行检验。

Abstract: Hidden-state probes often recover latent labels in imperfect-information sequence models, but this alone does not establish that a model maintains a posterior belief distribution over hidden states. This paper studies this ambiguity in a no-range Limit Hold'em autoregressive model trained only on action and value targets, not on an opponent's hand or range. Opponent-range probes are positive after action/value controls in two of three seeds, and the behavior head predicts held-out actions about five percentage points above a baseline using only observable public history. However, visible public betting composition explains more opponent-range signal than residual hidden states, suggesting that most recoverable information comes from betting summaries. Action/value+composition baselines reach 16.5-16.7% top-10 accuracy while composition-residual hidden probes fall to 11.4-12.2%, and matched-composition comparisons are negative in every seed. We call this evidence pattern composition-bounded predictive support: hidden states remain behavior-predictive and opponent-range correlated, but most recoverable range information is explained by visible betting composition rather than residual hidden-state structure. This is a case-study claim about opponent-range representational evidence, not exact Bayesian posterior tracking or a causal belief mechanism. Synthetic control and oracle validations show that the same diagnostics accept posterior-sensitive states and reject raw composition states under matched controls. Thus positive belief probes should be interpreted through targeted alternatives before being treated as evidence of belief tracking.

</details>


### [152] [Mitigating Scaffolding Collapse in Socratic Tutors via Representation Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19371)
*Jing Shao,Qifeng Wu,Hanyu Zhang,Sixia Sun,Jun Zhuang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种两阶段框架（Scaffold-Preserving Representation Alignment），通过监督微调预热+轨迹加权偏好优化+边界保持表示损失，防止基于LLM的苏格拉底式导师在多轮对话中因学生持续施压而放弃引导性提问、直接给出答案的“脚手架坍塌”问题。在5个STEM学科和5种对抗攻击策略上，该方法将Qwen3-8B的坍塌率降至32%，平均坍塌轮次推迟至9轮以上，且过度拒绝率较低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于LLM的苏格拉底式导师在多轮对话中，面对学生的持续施压（如反复要求直接答案），会逐渐放弃引导性提问而直接揭示解决方案，即“脚手架坍塌”问题。现有防御方法主要通过提示、偏好优化或过滤来约束可观测的输出行为，但未解决轨迹层面坍塌之前就发生的内部表示漂移问题。

Method: 两阶段框架：1) 用监督微调预热苏格拉底式导师；2) 结合轨迹加权直接偏好优化（trajectory-weighted DPO）和边界保持表示损失（margin-preserving representation loss），以冻结的参考状态为锚点，保持脚手架保持状态与坍塌诱导状态之间的隐藏状态分离。

Result: 在Qwen3-8B上，将坍塌率降至32%，平均坍塌轮次推迟至9轮以上，过度拒绝率保持较低水平。实验覆盖5个STEM学科和5种红队攻击策略。

Conclusion: 表示层面的对齐能够提高长程苏格拉底式导师在红队测试协议下的鲁棒性，有效缓解脚手架坍塌问题。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based Socratic tutors increasingly guide students through multi-turn questioning, but they can suffer from scaffolding collapse: under sustained student pressure, a tutor gradually abandons guided inquiry and reveals solutions directly. Prior defenses primarily constrain observable responses through prompting, preference optimization, or filtering, leaving the internal representation drift that precedes trajectory-level collapse largely unaddressed. We propose Scaffold-Preserving Representation Alignment, a two-stage framework that first warms up a Socratic tutor with supervised fine-tuning, then combines trajectory-weighted direct preference optimization with a margin-preserving representation loss anchored to frozen reference states. Our method is designed to maintain separation between scaffold-preserving and collapse-inducing hidden states across dialogue turns. We evaluate our method across five STEM disciplines and five red-teaming attack strategies. On Qwen3-8B, our method lowers Collapse Rate to 32%, delays average collapse onset beyond nine turns, and keeps over-refusal low, suggesting that representation-level alignment can improve the robustness of long-horizon Socratic tutoring under our red-teaming protocol.

### [153] [Euclean: Automated Geometry Problem Formalization with Unified Verification in Lean](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19374)
*Linbin Tang,Jingyan You,Zilin Kang,Hanzhang Liu,Sophia Zhang,Zenan Li,Chenrui Cao,Liangcheng Song,Jiaao Wu,Xian Zhang,Fan Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Euclean是一个四阶段框架，用于将几何问题自动形式化为原生Mathlib代码，解决了现有几何形式化系统碎片化、与Mathlib不兼容的问题，并构建了最大的Lean几何形式化数据集（OMNI-Geometry 768题，Numina-Geometry 177,597题），在人类评估中达到48.89% TOP1准确率，训练Goedel v2将证明成功率从13.6%提升至15.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有形式化推理系统存在碎片化问题：代数和数论用Lean处理，而几何仍依赖领域特定语言且缺乏形式化保证，这增加了可信计算基础并阻碍了统一模型开发。已有的Lean几何形式化工作（LeanEuclid, LeanGeo）使用与标准Mathlib不兼容的自定义公理系统，且规模小（<1,100题），限制了大规模训练。

Method: 提出Euclean四阶段框架：1) 约束显式化（Constraint Explication）——将隐含的图示假设（如拓扑配置和非退化条件）显式化；2) 配置锚定（Configuration Anchoring）——锚定几何配置；3) 形式化映射（Formalization Mapping）——将几何问题映射到Mathlib形式化表示；4) 迭代修复（Iterative Repair）——自动修复形式化过程中的错误。
